NOTE: PROCEDURE PRINTTO used (Total process time):
      real time           0.00 seconds
      cpu time            0.00 seconds
      

1394  proc donorimputation
1395     data=indata
1396     instatus=instat
1397     out=outdata
1398     outstatus=outstat
1399     donormap=map
1400     edits="Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 = T;"
1401     postedits="Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 >= 0.98*T; Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 <= 1.02*T;"
1402     mindonors=1
1403     pcentdonors=1
1404     n=100
1405     eligdon=any
1406     matchfieldstat
1407     seed=1
1408     acceptnegative
1409     ;
1410     id ident;
1411     mustmatch E;
1412     by Area;
1413  run;

NOTE: --- Banff System 2.08.002 developed by Statistics Canada ---
NOTE: PROCEDURE DONORIMPUTATION Version 2.06.002
NOTE: Created on Jan 19 2022 at 13:40:59
NOTE: Email: banff@statcan.gc.ca
NOTE: 

NOTE: DATA = WORK.INDATA
NOTE: INSTATUS = WORK.INSTAT
NOTE: OUT = WORK.OUTDATA
NOTE: OUTSTATUS = WORK.OUTSTAT
NOTE: DONORMAP = WORK.MAP
NOTE: EDITS = Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 = T;
NOTE: POSTEDITS = Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 >= 0.98*T; Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 <= 1.02*T;
NOTE: MINDONORS = 1
NOTE: PCENTDONORS = 1.00%
NOTE: N = 100
NOTE: NLIMIT not specified.
NOTE: MRL not specified.
NOTE: ELIGDON = ANY
NOTE: RANDOM not specified (random search of donors will not be performed)
NOTE: MATCHFIELDSTAT
NOTE: SEED = 1
NOTE: ACCEPTNEGATIVE
NOTE: DISPLAYLEVEL = 0
NOTE: ID = IDENT
NOTE: DATAEXCLVAR not specified.
NOTE: RANDNUMVAR not specified.
NOTE: MUSTMATCH = E 
NOTE: BY = Area 


Set of EDITS: 

0
                                      Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 - T   = 0


Set of POSTEDITS:

0
                             - Q1 - Q2 - Q3 - Q4 + 0.98 * T  <= 0

1
                               Q1 + Q2 + Q3 + Q4 - 1.02 * T  <= 0

NOTE: The minimal set of edits is equivalent to the original set of edits specified.

NOTE: The minimal set of post imputation edits is equivalent to the original set of edits 
      specified.

WARNING: BY variable Area is not on input data set WORK.INSTAT.

NOTE: This procedure can perform faster if the INSTATUS data set contains the BY 
      variables.
